INNER JOIN "Stations" AS "s0" ON "j"."ToStationId" = "s0"."Id"
WHERE "j"."FromStationId" = @__fromId_0 AND "j"."ToStationId" = @__toId_1 AND "j"."Departure" >= @__date_Date_2 AND "j"."Departure" < @__AddDays_3
ORDER BY "j"."Departure"
